     296             : void PrintDASHUsage()
     297             : {
     298           2 :         fprintf(stderr, "DASH Options:\n"
     299             :                 " -mpd m3u8            converts HLS manifest (local or remote http) to MPD \n"
     300             :                 "                       Note: not compatible with other DASH options (except -out and -tmp) and does not convert associated segments\n"
     301             :                 " -dash dur            enables DASH-ing of the file(s) with a segment duration of DUR ms\n"
     302             :                 "                       Note: the duration of a fragment (subsegment) is set\n"
     303             :                 "                              using the -frag switch.\n"
     304             :                 "                       Note: for onDemand profile, sets duration of a subsegment\n"
     305             :                 " -dash-strict dur     enables DASH-ing of the file(s) with a segment duration of DUR ms (old behaviour)\n"
     306             :                 "                       Note: the duration will be the closest to \'dur\', and will remain constant\n"
     307             :                 " -dash-live[=F] dur   generates a live DASH session using dur segment duration, optionally writing live context to F\n"
     308             :                 "                       MP4Box will run the live session until \'q\' is pressed or a fatal error occurs.\n"
     309             :                 " -ddbg-live[=F] dur   same as -dash-live without time regulation for debug purposes.\n"
     310             :                 " -frag time_in_ms     Specifies a fragment duration of time_in_ms.\n"
     311             :                 "                       * Note: By default, this is the DASH duration\n"
     312             :                 " -out filename        specifies output MPD file name.\n"
     313             :                 " -tmp dirname         specifies directory for temporary file creation\n"
     314             :                 "                       * Note: Default temp dir is OS-dependent\n"
     315             :                 " -profile NAME        specifies the target DASH profile: \"onDemand\",\n"
     316             :                 "                       \"live\", \"main\", \"simple\", \"full\",\n"
     317             :                 "                       \"hbbtv1.5:live\", \"dashavc264:live\", \"dashavc264:onDemand\"\n"
     318             :                 "                       * This will set default option values to ensure conformance to the desired profile\n"
     319             :                 "                       * Default profile is \"full\" in static mode, \"live\" in dynamic mode\n"
     320             :                 " -profile-ext STRING  specifies a list of profile extensions, as used by DASH-IF and DVB.\n"
     321             :                 "                       The string will be colon-concatenated with the profile used\n"
     322             :                 "\n"
     323             :                 "Input media files to dash can use the following modifiers\n"
     324             :                 " \"#trackID=N\"       only uses the track ID N from the source file\n"
     325             :                 " \"#video\"           only uses the first video track from the source file\n"
     326             :                 " \"#audio\"           only uses the first video track from the source file\n"
     327             :                 " \":id=NAME\"         sets the representation ID to NAME\n"
     328             :                 " \":dur=VALUE\"       processes VALUE seconds from the media\n"
     329             :                 "                       If VALUE is longer than the media duration, the last media duration is lengthen.\n"
     330             :                 " \":period=NAME\"     sets the representation's period to NAME. Multiple periods may be used\n"
     331             :                 "                       period appear in the MPD in the same order as specified with this option\n"
     332             :                 " \":BaseURL=NAME\"    sets the BaseURL. Set multiple times for multiple BaseURLs\n"
     333             :                 " \":bandwidth=VALUE\" sets the representation's bandwidth to a given value\n"
     334             :                 " \":period_duration=VALUE\"  increases the duration of this period by the given duration in seconds\n"
     335             :                 "                       only used when no input media is specified (remote period insertion), eg :period=X:xlink=Z:duration=Y.\n"
     336             :                 " \":xlink=VALUE\"     sets the xlink value for the period containing this element\n"
     337             :                 "                       only the xlink declared on the first rep of a period will be used\n"
     338             :                 " \":role=VALUE\"      sets the role of this representation (cf DASH spec).\n"
     339             :                 "                       media with different roles belong to different adaptation sets.\n"
     340             :                 " \":desc_p=VALUE\"    adds a descriptor at the Period level. Value must be a properly formatted XML element.\n"
     341             :                 " \":desc_as=VALUE\"   adds a descriptor at the AdaptationSet level. Value must be a properly formatted XML element.\n"
     342             :                 "                       two input files with different values will be in different AdaptationSet elements.\n"
     343             :                 " \":desc_as_c=VALUE\" adds a descriptor at the AdaptationSet level. Value must be a properly formatted XML element.\n"
     344             :                 "                       value is ignored while creating AdaptationSet elements.\n"
     345             :                 " \":desc_rep=VALUE\"  adds a descriptor at the Representation level. Value must be a properly formatted XML element.\n"
     346             :                 "                       value is ignored while creating AdaptationSet elements.\n"
     347             :                 "\n"
     348             :                 " -rap                 segments begin with random access points\n"
     349             :                 "                       Note: segment duration may not be exactly what asked by\n"
     350             :                 "                       \"-dash\" since encoded video data is not modified\n"
     351             :                 " -frag-rap            All fragments begin with random access points\n"
     352             :                 "                       Note: fragment duration may not be exactly what is asked by\n"
     353             :                 "                       \"-frag\" since encoded video data is not modified\n"
     354             :                 " -segment-name name   sets the segment name for generated segments\n"
     355             :                 "                       If not set (default), segments are concatenated in output file\n"
     356             :                 "                        except in \"live\" profile where dash_%%s is used\n"
     357             :                 " -segment-ext name    sets the segment extension. Default is m4s, \"null\" means no extension\n"
     358             :                 " -segment-timeline    uses SegmentTimeline when generating segments.\n"
     359             :                 " -segment-marker MARK adds a box of type \'MARK\' at the end of each DASH segment. MARK shall be a 4CC identifier\n"
     360             :                 " -insert-utc          inserts UTC clock at the begining of each ISOBMF segment\n"
     361             :                 " -base-url string     sets Base url at MPD level. Can be used several times.\n"
     362             :                 " -mpd-title string    sets MPD title.\n"
     363             :                 " -mpd-source string   sets MPD source.\n"
     364             :                 " -mpd-info-url string sets MPD info url.\n"
     365             :                 " -cprt string         adds copyright string to MPD\n"
     366             :                 " -dash-ctx FILE       stores/restore DASH timing from FILE.\n"
     367             :                 " -dynamic             uses dynamic MPD type instead of static.\n"
     368             :                 " -last-dynamic        same as dynamic but closes the period (insert lmsg brand if needed and update duration).\n"
     369             :                 " -mpd-duration DUR    sets the duration in second of a live session (0 by default). If 0, you must use -mpd-refresh.\n"
     370             :                 " -mpd-refresh TIME    specifies MPD update time in seconds (double can be used).\n"
     371             :                 " -time-shift  TIME    specifies MPD time shift buffer depth in seconds (default 0). Specify -1 to keep all files\n"
     372             :                 " -subdur DUR          specifies maximum duration in ms of the input file to be dashed in LIVE or context mode.\n"
     373             :                 "                       NOTE: This does not change the segment duration: dashing stops once segments produced exceeded the duration.\n"
     374             :                 " -min-buffer TIME     specifies MPD min buffer time in milliseconds\n"
     375             :                 " -ast-offset TIME     specifies MPD AvailabilityStartTime offset in ms if positive, or availabilityTimeOffset of each representation if negative. Default is 0 sec delay\n"
     376             :                 " -dash-scale SCALE    specifies that timing for -dash and -frag are expressed in SCALE units per seconds\n"
     377             :                 " -mem-frags           fragments will be produced in memory rather than on disk before flushing to disk\n"
     378             :                 " -pssh-moof           stores PSSH boxes in first moof of each segments. By default PSSH are stored in movie box.\n"
     379             :                 " -sample-groups-traf  stores sample group descriptions in traf (duplicated for each traf) rather than in moof. By default sample group descriptions are stored in movie box.\n"
     380             : 
     381             :                 "\n"
     382             :                 "Advanced Options, should not be needed when using -profile:\n"
     383             :                 " -subsegs-per-sidx N  sets the number of subsegments to be written in each SIDX box\n"
     384             :                 "                       If 0, a single SIDX box is used per segment\n"
     385             :                 "                       If -1, no SIDX box is used\n"
     386             :                 " -url-template        uses SegmentTemplate instead of explicit sources in segments.\n"
     387             :                 "                       Ignored if segments are stored in the output file.\n"
     388             :                 " -daisy-chain         uses daisy-chain SIDX instead of hierarchical. Ignored if frags/sidx is 0.\n"
     389             :                 " -single-segment      uses a single segment for the whole file (OnDemand profile). \n"
     390             :                 " -single-file         uses a single file for the whole file (default). \n"
     391             :                 " -bs-switching MODE   sets bitstream switching to \"inband\" (default), \"merge\", \"multi\", \"no\" or \"single\" to test with single input.\n"
     392             :                 " -moof-sn N           sets sequence number of first moof to N\n"
     393             :                 " -tfdt N              sets TFDT of first traf to N in SCALE units (cf -dash-scale)\n"
     394             :                 " -no-frags-default    disables default flags in fragments\n"
     395             :                 " -single-traf         uses a single track fragment per moof (smooth streaming and derived specs may require this)\n"
     396             :                 " -dash-ts-prog N      program_number to be considered in case of an MPTS input file.\n"
     397             :                 " -frag-rt             when using fragments in live mode, flush fragments according to their timing (only supported with a single input).\n"
     398             :                 " -cp-location=MODE    sets ContentProtection element location. Possible values for mode are:\n"
     399             :                 "                        as: sets ContentProtection in AdaptationSet element\n"
     400             :                 "                        rep: sets ContentProtection in Representation element\n"
